title:SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide
description:This guide is meant for finding what makes each weapon unique; a roll that only this weapon can get. It is largely meant for veteran players who already have a solid number of good rolls of multiple weapons. There are certain great combinations that multiple weapons can roll (e.g. Outlaw+Kill Clip) that should be considered always “good rolls” regardless of the advice given here. Also, for the most part the guide will be generally about PvE. I’ve pulled information across time from sources like Pandapaxxy, Mercules, Ehroar, Fallout Plays, CoolGuy, Legoleflash, Aegis, and other streamer and community resources. And lastly, I’m pulling from my own meandering experience. Below a bolded perk means that it is something that I personally will be looking for and that I believe are the best perks for the gun (remembering that I tend to focus on high-end PvE). Unbolded perks are either PvP-focused or simply perks that are good, but not my personal choices.

//SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c)  "" Masterwork: 



title:Pale Heart Craftable Weapons
description:The origin trait for these weapons is called Dealer’s Choice and it grants super energy on kills. The amount stacks with the number of Dealer’s Choice weapons you use. Think of it as Thresh for free. It is a fine perk and can mostly just be ignored as “free real estate”. However, this season’s artifact has a perk called Winning Hand which makes your Dealer’s Choice weapons cause solar explosions on kills - again stacking with multiple. This perk makes these weapons huge overperformers this season - expect them to come down to earth in 4 months.

// Bold Endings ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "Rare archetype and one of two added this season. The stats are quite good compared to the rest of the archetype, but kinda brutal compared to other hand cannons. The reload has to be addressed, especially since you’re going to be super tempted to take Headstone in column 1 over Rapid Hit. In general this should be a pretty cool weapon, especially this season, but we’ve had a similar gun in the game for awhile now (Something New) and it hasn’t really picked up a following, so after the season this may suffer a similar fate." Masterwork: Reload

// No Hesitation ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "The first and only support-frame auto in the game. A very cool weapon that allows you to heal your allies and also be able to perform the role of a standard primary. The base stats of the gun are so high that it basically does not need help in any category, so we may as well boost range or just pump stats to the sky. In terms of perks it may seem like Physic and Circle of Life are both “duh” for a weapon that wants to heal your team - and that is probably true for any build that isn’t dedicated to healing already (basically any class with access to healing grenade) - however, the gun already heals allies as a base function, so you don’t need a perk in order to access that capability. In general, if a player is being actively healed and dies anyway there probably wasn’t any amount of healing you could have provided that would have saved them. That’s why my recommendation is actually skewed more toward making the gun at base more useful on its own and synergize with your build rather than overindexing into the healing aspect. Demo gives you more access to healing grenade which imo does a better job at being a healbot when you want to than Physic will. Incandescent is so powerful at base that it is really hard to not take it. Circle of Life may be more powerful in high-end content, but the jury is still out on that. This weapon is a 100% definite craft." Masterwork: Reload
dimwishlist:item=1801007332&perks=4090651448,3230963543,3523296417,4293542123

// Someday (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "Hail to the King! Absolute PvP powerhouse. This has superior stats in every category to Matador (and all other precision shotguns) while having the exact same god roll - and you can craft exactly the roll you want. This allows you to thread the needle with your stat setup to hit exactly 100 range with opening shot without needing to overindex into range. Tons of handling, just an absolute beast. The only thing you can knock it for is sharing a slot with Conditional Finality. For PvE there is one good use case using Recombination similar to Heritage, and this time without needing a precision hit - making this far more usable in general and high-end content. The downside is that it does not have an autoloading perk and manually reloading shotguns sucks." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve
dimwishlist:item=3232203524&perks=1300023272,791862061,4071163871,469285294

// Axial Lacuna ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "Stats here are middle of the pack, and the archetype is one of the weaker ones for PvE. The gun can get a very good perk pairing for PvE, but it is basically almost identical to the Techeun Force roll and that doesn’t really see much play. As far as solar fusions go this may be on par with a Vorpal Cartesian for DPS/bursting and/or a Reservoir Burst Royal Execution for general play. It fits in snugly between both of those and maye ultimately carve out a niche, but for the most part solar fusions just don’t really see play in the current meta." Masterwork: Handling

// The Call ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "This archetype is so busted it doesn’t even matter what the stats or perks are tbh. ANY roll of these weapons is great, and if you get good perks and stats then it’s just gravy. In terms of perks you want a healthy balance of reload and blast radius, with velocity being a decent fill-in. That being said, this is one of the most “dealer’s choice” (pun very much intended) of all the rocket-sidearms since there is no definite best perk here in either column, and it can largely just come down to user preference. Slice or Lead from Gold are going to be the general consensus perks for high-end content, and Subsistence working for players who are using it in more general play or are going double special in high-end content using this gun for add clear. Demolitionist + Adrenaline Junkie is also on the gun in the perk 1 slot if that is more your speed. The two main column 2 perks I’d recommend are either Vorpal or One for All depending on your playstyle. If you want to just whip the gun out and hammer down a mini-boss/ultra/champ with it as fast as possible then definitely go with Vorpal. If you want to main the weapon and use it more generally for add clear then One for All would be more suitable for that." Masterwork: Blast Radius
dimwishlist:item=3947966653&perks=1478423395,3230963543,923806249,1546637391


// The Call ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks "This archetype is so busted it doesn’t even matter what the stats or perks are tbh. ANY roll of these weapons is great, and if you get good perks and stats then it’s just gravy. In terms of perks you want a healthy balance of reload and blast radius, with velocity being a decent fill-in. That being said, this is one of the most “dealer’s choice” (pun very much intended) of all the rocket-sidearms since there is no definite best perk here in either column, and it can largely just come down to user preference. Slice or Lead from Gold are going to be the general consensus perks for high-end content, and Subsistence working for players who are using it in more general play or are going double special in high-end content using this gun for add clear. Demolitionist + Adrenaline Junkie is also on the gun in the perk 1 slot if that is more your speed. The two main column 2 perks I’d recommend are either Vorpal or One for All depending on your playstyle. If you want to just whip the gun out and hammer down a mini-boss/ultra/champ with it as fast as possible then definitely go with Vorpal. If you want to main the weapon and use it more generally for add clear then One for All would be more suitable for that." Masterwork: Blast Radius, Reload

dimwishlist:item=4195186942&perks=3525010810,3796465595,3300816228,3194351027



title:Salvation’s Edge Craftable Weapons
description:The origin trait for these weapons is called Collective Purpose. It basically just grants some small QoL buffs to weapons that scales based on the number of allies near you. This is a nice bonus, but nothing that inherently makes these desirable on its own. The real “origin trait” here is the existence of the raid weapon-specific perk Chaos Reshaped. This grants 20% damage after 12 seconds in combat (same trigger condition as Frenzy, but 5% more damage instead of maxed Handling and Reload). The real kicker is that after another 12 seconds that bonus goes all the way up to 35%. This is a fantastic perk for high-end content and should be the main reason for chasing these guns.

// Critical Anomaly ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "The best kinetic slot sniper rifle not named The Supremacy, despite the mediocre archetype. The real trick is going to be finding content to use it in, but wherever you find that content this should be good. For the most part you are just using this as part of a DPS rotation, and the real tradeoff is whether you can guarantee to keep up CR heading into DPS, because as soon as it comes off it will fall way behind a Firing Line Irukandji." Masterwork: Handling

// Nullify ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "Another new archetype and one of three introduced this season - this one being the only solar version. Despite being a raid weapon, this actually does not have the best stats in the archetype, but that’s less important since the main comparisons to draw are actually going to be with Adhortative, Darkest Before, and BxR Battler. The only roll this can’t get that those can is the Attrition Orbs+Incandescent roll, but this gets so much else it is hard to not roll with this gun. Off the bat Incandescent is the likely choice in the 2nd column, but Chaos Reshaped is a 20-35% damage increase in higher-end content plus some incidental healing that is hard to shrug off. Firefly is fun, but falls off at higher levels and doesn’t synergize super well with Incandescent. Demolitionist combos extremely well with Incandescent, and I would be remiss not to mention Under-Over for this season for stunning champions. There are a lot of ways to build this and all of them should be good. Very cool and very exciting gun." Masterwork: Reload

// Nullify () (Adept)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "Another new archetype and one of three introduced this season - this one being the only solar version. Despite being a raid weapon, this actually does not have the best stats in the archetype, but that’s less important since the main comparisons to draw are actually going to be with Adhortative, Darkest Before, and BxR Battler. The only roll this can’t get that those can is the Attrition Orbs+Incandescent roll, but this gets so much else it is hard to not roll with this gun. Off the bat Incandescent is the likely choice in the 2nd column, but Chaos Reshaped is a 20-35% damage increase in higher-end content plus some incidental healing that is hard to shrug off. Firefly is fun, but falls off at higher levels and doesn’t synergize super well with Incandescent. Demolitionist combos extremely well with Incandescent, and I would be remiss not to mention Under-Over for this season for stunning champions. There are a lot of ways to build this and all of them should be good. Very cool and very exciting gun." Masterwork: Reload
dimwishlist:item=892183998&perks=839105230,3230963543,3017780555,4293542123

// Maahes HC4 ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "Rare archetype and one of two added this season. The stats here are the worst across the board for the archetype and it is a random roll, so you’re going to have trouble shoring up its weaknesses without some luck. The good news is that there are very few good void primary weapons in the game, especially hand cannons, so this doesn’t have much competition. The main comparison is Word of Crota, so a lot of the value is going to be just straight up preference since these weapons are on the opposite side of the spectrum in terms of feel." Masterwork: Reload
dimwishlist:item=1246793994&perks=1840239774,3230963543,776531651,4104185692


// Maahes HC4 ()

The stats here are the worst across the board for the archetype and it is a random roll, so you’re going to have trouble shoring up its weaknesses without some luck. The good news is that there are very few good void primary weapons in the game, especially hand cannons, so this doesn’t have much competition. The main comparison is Word of Crota, so a lot of the value is going to be just straight up preference since these weapons are on the opposite side of the spectrum in terms of feel." // Ergo Sum ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommend Perks first choice "This is a weird one to evaluate, but I’ll give it a shot. For the most part, you want a Wolfpack Rounds Ergo Sum for group sword DPS. There are 2 ways to think about which frame is best, with Caster being about to more reliably proc the Pack Hunter buff from anywhere, and with the Lightweight frame being the quickest way. Outside of that use case, Arc Conductor (Riskrunner) is a cool way to get some guaranteed resistance and add clear on demand, and Unplanned Reprieve (Telesto) seems like it might be a decent way to add some extra damage to a sword rotation this season with both Argent Blade and Expanding Abyss artifact perks." Exotic Perk: Wolfpack Rounds
dimwishlist:item=1681583613&perks=1261178282,269888150,519046634

// Whisper of the Worm ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "The biggest thing here is that A) you want as much ammo as possible - so Field Prep is great especially for gathering ammo between damage phases and not just at really flag, and B) you don’t want to miss - so No Distractions makes sense for that. Between the two I’d tend to lean toward the ammo and then try to shore up stability in the rest of the gun to help with flinch resist. Handling is a great stat to have on snipers in general as well." Masterwork:

title:Into the Light BRAVE Arsenal Random Roll Weapons
description:The Origin trait here is called Indomitability which grants grenade energy on kills with a Light subclass equipped or melee energy likewise with a Dark subclass. In general this sounds like a pretty good origin trait as it is basically mini-Demolitionist/Pugilist for free. It won’t really alter the usage or stats on these weapons, but it’s a pretty cool selling point and makes these weapons valuable beyond just their base perk and stat packages.

// Forbearance ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "Another weird choice to bring back as the origin trait on the original version is far better than this one, but it isn’t all bad as this version can be reborn with a new ability-battery identity. Using the origin trait as a starting point you can add both Demo and Wellspring to the gun to have massive ability regen. You can also get the original god roll of Ambitious Assassin + Chain Reaction here as well. And if you’re feeling like speculating on the market you can try investing in some damage perks that may overtake Chain Reaction once The Final Shape (and subsequent Chain Reaction nerf) is upon us. Overall I’m calling this #10 in priority for now." Masterwork: Reload

// The Mountaintop (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls first choice "WOW. The madlads actually did it. This is one of the absolute most exciting weapons they’ve ever brought into the game. It has lightweight bonuses, fires in a straight line (basically a sniper rifle), now allows you to grenade jump (shoot at your feet to boost yourself), and does incredible damage. This archetype is also breaking rules regarding stats. On specifically just this weapon you want to try to drop your blast radius as far as you can, and Spike Grenades are also good. The perks are also just completely insane. Recombination should be completely insane for damage rotations as well as general play for bursting down majors. Frenzy deserves a shoutout for use in damage rotations or paired with Ambitious Assassin if you’d prefer to main the weapon. Vorpal may have some limited use in damage rotations, but should be worse than other options. Sticky Grenades is just an extra mobility option as you can stand on the grenades to climb into weird locations (at least you used to be able to, so I assume you still can). If it wasn’t for one other weapon being even more insane than this and only available in a limited capacity (just these 2 months) this would be the undisputed chase weapon. As it stands this is #2 in priority." Masterwork: Handling tags:god-pve

// Edge Transit (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls first choice "Still probably on par with if not better than Cataphract due to enhanced perks. You want a mag-boosting perk (either Augmented Drum or Mini Frags) paired with Backup Mag to use during the Envious Assassin add clear phase to boost the mag up to almost all of your reserves shifted over to the one overflowed mag before swapping over to Spike Grenades, or even just something that boosts velocity. Deconstruct is also performing well when paired with the Sticky Grenades mag perk since it only takes 2 direct hits to trigger the ammo refund from Deconstruct. This means you gain essentially 50% extra total damage across your reserves, assuming you’re in a situation where you can’t easily get more heavy ammo through other means and you’re in a long encounter with a lot of necessitated heavy weapon usage. It’s a pretty niche use case that most players will not usually get much value from, since in most cases you’re using the GL for its DPS value, not for total damage, so you’d be much happier with Bait & Switch or even Explosive Light in most cases. Lastly, do not pair Deconstruct with Envious Assassin, it is an anti-combo as the ammo refund can’t trigger when the mag is above its starting point. On top of all of this you can get pretty good PvP rolls as well, where you want as much Blast Radius as you can possibly get. Easily the #1 chase priority." Masterwork: Handling tags:god-pve

// Edge Transit (god-pvp)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvP Recommend Rolls first choice "Still probably on par with if not better than Cataphract due to enhanced perks. You want a mag-boosting perk (either Augmented Drum or Mini Frags) paired with Backup Mag to use during the Envious Assassin add clear phase to boost the mag up to almost all of your reserves shifted over to the one overflowed mag before swapping over to Spike Grenades, or even just something that boosts velocity. Deconstruct is also performing well when paired with the Sticky Grenades mag perk since it only takes 2 direct hits to trigger the ammo refund from Deconstruct. This means you gain essentially 50% extra total damage across your reserves, assuming you’re in a situation where you can’t easily get more heavy ammo through other means and you’re in a long encounter with a lot of necessitated heavy weapon usage. It’s a pretty niche use case that most players will not usually get much value from, since in most cases you’re using the GL for its DPS value, not for total damage, so you’d be much happier with Bait & Switch or even Explosive Light in most cases. Lastly, do not pair Deconstruct with Envious Assassin, it is an anti-combo as the ammo refund can’t trigger when the mag is above its starting point. On top of all of this you can get pretty good PvP rolls as well, where you want as much Blast Radius as you can possibly get. Easily the #1 chase priority." Masterwork: Blast Radius tags:god-pvp
dimwishlist:item=568611923&perks=1478423395,1380253176,951095735,3993379141


// Edge Transit (pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls "Still probably on par with if not better than Cataphract due to enhanced perks. You want a mag-boosting perk (either Augmented Drum or Mini Frags) paired with Backup Mag to use during the Envious Assassin add clear phase to boost the mag up to almost all of your reserves shifted over to the one overflowed mag before swapping over to Spike Grenades, or even just something that boosts velocity. Deconstruct is also performing well when paired with the Sticky Grenades mag perk since it only takes 2 direct hits to trigger the ammo refund from Deconstruct. This means you gain essentially 50% extra total damage across your reserves, assuming you’re in a situation where you can’t easily get more heavy ammo through other means and you’re in a long encounter with a lot of necessitated heavy weapon usage. It’s a pretty niche use case that most players will not usually get much value from, since in most cases you’re using the GL for its DPS value, not for total damage, so you’d be much happier with Bait & Switch or even Explosive Light in most cases. Lastly, do not pair Deconstruct with Envious Assassin, it is an anti-combo as the ammo refund can’t trigger when the mag is above its starting point. On top of all of this you can get pretty good PvP rolls as well, where you want as much Blast Radius as you can possibly get. Easily the #1 chase priority." // Edge Transit (pvp)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvP Recommend Rolls "Still probably on par with if not better than Cataphract due to enhanced perks. You want a mag-boosting perk (either Augmented Drum or Mini Frags) paired with Backup Mag to use during the Envious Assassin add clear phase to boost the mag up to almost all of your reserves shifted over to the one overflowed mag before swapping over to Spike Grenades, or even just something that boosts velocity. Deconstruct is also performing well when paired with the Sticky Grenades mag perk since it only takes 2 direct hits to trigger the ammo refund from Deconstruct. This means you gain essentially 50% extra total damage across your reserves, assuming you’re in a situation where you can’t easily get more heavy ammo through other means and you’re in a long encounter with a lot of necessitated heavy weapon usage. It’s a pretty niche use case that most players will not usually get much value from, since in most cases you’re using the GL for its DPS value, not for total damage, so you’d be much happier with Bait & Switch or even Explosive Light in most cases. Lastly, do not pair Deconstruct with Envious Assassin, it is an anti-combo as the ammo refund can’t trigger when the mag is above its starting point. On top of all of this you can get pretty good PvP rolls as well, where you want as much Blast Radius as you can possibly get. Easily the #1 chase priority." Masterwork: Blast Radius tags:pvp

// The Recluse (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "The hype for this returning former juggernaut has died down a lot, but it should still be the best void submachine gun if you can get your hands on the right roll. Enlightened Action + Desperate Measures or Surrounded (especially good in Onslaught) for a general use weapon, or Repulsor Brace + Frenzy for Gyrfalcon Hunter. Desperate Measures seems to fall off really easily if you have volatile rounds on your weapon, so I would not recommend using that on Gyrfalcon. Due to its BiS categorization this picks up a #5 priority." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve

// The Recluse (pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks "The hype for this returning former juggernaut has died down a lot, but it should still be the best void submachine gun if you can get your hands on the right roll. Enlightened Action + Desperate Measures or Surrounded (especially good in Onslaught) for a general use weapon, or Repulsor Brace + Frenzy for Gyrfalcon Hunter. Desperate Measures seems to fall off really easily if you have volatile rounds on your weapon, so I would not recommend using that on Gyrfalcon. Due to its BiS categorization this picks up a #5 priority." Masterwork: Reload, Range tags:pve

// Hung Jury SR4 (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls first choice "Oh look. It’s back again. For some reason. Yay? And oof, they put the PvE  god roll of Shoot to Loot + Kinetic Tremors in the same column so you can’t get it on this one; so, right away this version of Hung Jury is strictly worse than the last Nightfall version for that reason. You can get Tremors + Firefly which is somewhat interesting, but is definitely not worth using over the previous version of the gun. For PvP they left the Box Breathing roll just as is, so this gives everyone another chance to pick up that roll - which is absolute dynamite in the crucible. For me, having the Box Breathing god roll already this drops to the bottom of the priority list (#11), but if you don’t have the Box Breathing roll you can chase it." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve

// Falling Guillotine (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "Vortex frame swords are horrible for dps right now. The heavy attack is a net dps loss as it costs 6 ammo when 4 light swings are an equivalent amount of damage. You can get double damage perks on this, but without relentless strikes your total damage will absolutely plummet since you can’t print ammo while you attack. Like so many other swords before it, this weapon with Surrounded (even when enhanced in TFS) can’t compete with Bequest simply due to Bequest’s unnatural extra 10 impact stat it has over all other swords. However, Bequest is only the top dog if you can guarantee you have Surrounded proc’d. Once you lose that then things like The Lament start coming into play - and that’s where this sword might actually come through. As long as you’re sure you can completely eschew total damage (sacrificing Relentless Strikes in column 1 for a damage perk) then the straight DPS of Frenzy/Vorpal + Bait & Switch might be a legit meta DPS option for situations where you can’t proc surrounded (e.g. Caiatl in Duality dungeon). We can speculate for the future looking at a potential buff to vortex frames or swords in general and this weapon is all upside if that winds up being the case. It may be worth picking up a roll with double damage perks just in case these ever become meta again. Calling this #9 in priority." Masterwork: Impact tags:god-pve

// Hammerhead (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "I was really excited for this gun to come back and it came back strong in some ways and mediocre in others. As the standard “void MG” it cannot compete with Commemoration. Reconstruction + Killing Tally on that gun can’t be beaten by anything this gun can do. Rewind Rounds is a pale shadow of Reconstruction, Bray Inheritance is way stronger than Indomitability. However, this can roll double lethality perks in the forms of Rampage in column 1 plus Onslaught or Killing Tally in column 2. Specifically on Void Hunter, and Hunter in general for that matter, you can use dodge to bypass the truly odious reload time of a machine gun and maintain the massive damage capability of the double damage perks. Sadly, Hunter dodge will reset Killing Tally, but that’s not necessarily the end of the world. It can also get a pretty good counter-meta PvP roll as well. Overall this is my #8 chase priority weapon." Masterwork: Handling tags:god-pve

// Blast Furnace (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommended Perks first choice "Aggressive Bursts have been in a weird place for awhile in Destiny. The deterministic recoil on this weapon will be the main factor in whether or not this is usable in PvP. If it is usable this should wind up being a very solid gun, along the lines of a Belisarius-D. For PvE there is basically just one roll you’d be looking for with Kinetic Tremors and Frenzy, and that may very well be good enough to break into high-end content over the likes of a perfect Battle Scar. The combination of the QoL buffs and damage from Frenzy, the enhanced perks (once TFS launches), and the origin trait being better may all place this above a classic Shoot to Loot + Tremors pulse like Battle Scar. If you like the gun it should be a fun nostalgic weapon to pick up and use. #6 priority, middle of the pack." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve

// Elsie's Rifle (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "Tough weapon to judge for PvE. On the surface it looks underwhelming, but there are some interesting perks in here to note. I should also note that this weapon has literally double the base reload of the rest of its archetype. 60 base reload is insane here and should not be overlooked. Perks-wise this has some ok perks for clearing low-level content like Desperate Measures, Kill Clip, and Adrenaline Junkie, but the fact that this is a void weapon hurts the use case for all of those due to subclass limitations. That leaves Frenzy as the premiere choice for high-end content and oh boy Under-Over and Repulsor Brace as pairings are super juicy here. Under-Over would be ideal for the next time we get an anti-barrier season and Repulsor Brace should be the far more ubiquitous choice for Gyrfalcon Hunter. Overall though this archetype isn’t really used much in PvE. For PvP this is an absolute monster of a weapon. Elsie’s can hit max range with the aid of Keep Away and looks like it could be very, very strong - unfortunately the deterministic recoil pattern is horrible on this weapon. Do not run a counterbalance mod, in any configuration it just pulls the recoil poorly. You need one of the 3 recoil-adjusting barrel perks to make this usable at all, preferably Extended Barrel being the premiere choice. The base stats on Elsie’s are huge. It’s like having a Messenger with 3 adept mods already on it (2 in reload, 1 in handling). Overall, this is looking like a great chase for PvP, so making it a #4 prio." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve

dimwishlist:item=2372514509&perks=1467527085,3230963543,1870851715,4104185692

// Midnight Coup ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "The return of one of the best weapons from Y1 of D2. They’ve buffed the base stat package here and juiced up the perk pool. This should supplant Fatebringer (even the timelost versions) as the premiere PvE kinetic slot handcannon for high-end content. Deterministic recoil here really sucks, and neither of the +10 barrels actually fixes it, so you’d just be looking for Arrowhead Brake. The biggest chase should be Shoot to Loot + Kinetic Tremors, but Attrition Orbs (the tremors count to attrition stacks) paired with Tremors is also a dynamite roll I’d suggest keeping as well. The weapon needs reload help at base to help it out. I’d recommend at least 71 (maybe 66) in reload stat, but you’d really be happy with 81. This makes the jump in reload from a Firefly proc fairly meaningless, and the actual damage from a firefly proc is pretty lackluster in a small radius (especially in high-end content), so even though people are going nuts over it I honestly wouldn’t recommend it. The best current roll then would be to go for either Explosive Payload + Frenzy or one of the Kinetic Tremors rolls mentioned above (EP, Attrition, or Shoot). For the classic Fatebringer roll (EP+Frenzy) this weapon has worse stats (Range & Stab since Frenzy maxes out Handling and Reload), but the perks can be enhanced and it has a pretty good origin trait compared to the rather meaningless adept mods that Fatebringer can get on its Timelost version. Without Arrowhead Brake though this weapon won’t feel as good as Fatebringer does. Tough to get a good roll on this since you need the perk combo AND reload help AND arrowhead brake. This is high priority (#3)." Masterwork: Reload

// Midnight Coup ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks "The return of one of the best weapons from Y1 of D2. They’ve buffed the base stat package here and juiced up the perk pool. This should supplant Fatebringer (even the timelost versions) as the premiere PvE kinetic slot handcannon for high-end content. Deterministic recoil here really sucks, and neither of the +10 barrels actually fixes it, so you’d just be looking for Arrowhead Brake. The biggest chase should be Shoot to Loot + Kinetic Tremors, but Attrition Orbs (the tremors count to attrition stacks) paired with Tremors is also a dynamite roll I’d suggest keeping as well. The weapon needs reload help at base to help it out. I’d recommend at least 71 (maybe 66) in reload stat, but you’d really be happy with 81. This makes the jump in reload from a Firefly proc fairly meaningless, and the actual damage from a firefly proc is pretty lackluster in a small radius (especially in high-end content), so even though people are going nuts over it I honestly wouldn’t recommend it. The best current roll then would be to go for either Explosive Payload + Frenzy or one of the Kinetic Tremors rolls mentioned above (EP, Attrition, or Shoot). For the classic Fatebringer roll (EP+Frenzy) this weapon has worse stats (Range & Stab since Frenzy maxes out Handling and Reload), but the perks can be enhanced and it has a pretty good origin trait compared to the rather meaningless adept mods that Fatebringer can get on its Timelost version. Without Arrowhead Brake though this weapon won’t feel as good as Fatebringer does. Tough to get a good roll on this since you need the perk combo AND reload help AND arrowhead brake. This is high priority (#3)." Masterwork: Reload

// Succession (god-pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "Oof. From the top to the bottom of these new weapons. There is actually no reason to get this gun at all. The raid version is strictly better in every way as this brings no better or more interesting perk pairings, and the Bray Inheritance origin trait is just a better version of Indomitability. The only thing that could be said here is that Discord is at least something different in perk slot 1, but you’d have to eschew Reconstruction for that, and ultimately what would be the point? I get that it prints free ammo, but why are you using an aggressive sniper rifle for add clear? This weapon makes no sense to reissue and should be the only hard avoid on the list. #12 and it isn’t close. " Masterwork: Handling tags:god-pve

// The Mountaintop (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls first choice "WOW. The madlads actually did it. This is one of the absolute most exciting weapons they’ve ever brought into the game. It has lightweight bonuses, fires in a straight line (basically a sniper rifle), now allows you to grenade jump (shoot at your feet to boost yourself), and does incredible damage. This archetype is also breaking rules regarding stats. On specifically just this weapon you want to try to drop your blast radius as far as you can, and Spike Grenades are also good. The perks are also just completely insane. Recombination should be completely insane for damage rotations as well as general play for bursting down majors. Frenzy deserves a shoutout for use in damage rotations or paired with Ambitious Assassin if you’d prefer to main the weapon. Vorpal may have some limited use in damage rotations, but should be worse than other options. Sticky Grenades is just an extra mobility option as you can stand on the grenades to climb into weird locations (at least you used to be able to, so I assume you still can). If it wasn’t for one other weapon being even more insane than this and only available in a limited capacity (just these 2 months) this would be the undisputed chase weapon. As it stands this is #2 in priority." Masterwork: Handling tags:god-pve
dimwishlist:item=4043921923&perks=981914802,3492396210,3300816228,469285294
dimwishlist:item=4043921923&perks=981914802,3301904089,3300816228,469285294


// The Mountaintop (pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls "WOW. The madlads actually did it. This is one of the absolute most exciting weapons they’ve ever brought into the game. It has lightweight bonuses, fires in a straight line (basically a sniper rifle), now allows you to grenade jump (shoot at your feet to boost yourself), and does incredible damage. This archetype is also breaking rules regarding stats. On specifically just this weapon you want to try to drop your blast radius as far as you can, and Spike Grenades are also good. The perks are also just completely insane. Recombination should be completely insane for damage rotations as well as general play for bursting down majors. Frenzy deserves a shoutout for use in damage rotations or paired with Ambitious Assassin if you’d prefer to main the weapon. Vorpal may have some limited use in damage rotations, but should be worse than other options. Sticky Grenades is just an extra mobility option as you can stand on the grenades to climb into weird locations (at least you used to be able to, so I assume you still can). If it wasn’t for one other weapon being even more insane than this and only available in a limited capacity (just these 2 months) this would be the undisputed chase weapon. As it stands this is #2 in priority." Masterwork: Handling, Velocity, Reload tags:pve

// Edge Transit (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls first choice "Still probably on par with if not better than Cataphract due to enhanced perks. You want a mag-boosting perk (either Augmented Drum or Mini Frags) paired with Backup Mag to use during the Envious Assassin add clear phase to boost the mag up to almost all of your reserves shifted over to the one overflowed mag before swapping over to Spike Grenades, or even just something that boosts velocity. Deconstruct is also performing well when paired with the Sticky Grenades mag perk since it only takes 2 direct hits to trigger the ammo refund from Deconstruct. This means you gain essentially 50% extra total damage across your reserves, assuming you’re in a situation where you can’t easily get more heavy ammo through other means and you’re in a long encounter with a lot of necessitated heavy weapon usage. It’s a pretty niche use case that most players will not usually get much value from, since in most cases you’re using the GL for its DPS value, not for total damage, so you’d be much happier with Bait & Switch or even Explosive Light in most cases. Lastly, do not pair Deconstruct with Envious Assassin, it is an anti-combo as the ammo refund can’t trigger when the mag is above its starting point. On top of all of this you can get pretty good PvP rolls as well, where you want as much Blast Radius as you can possibly get. Easily the #1 chase priority." Masterwork: Handling tags:god-pve

// Edge Transit (god-pvp) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvP Recommend Rolls first choice "Still probably on par with if not better than Cataphract due to enhanced perks. You want a mag-boosting perk (either Augmented Drum or Mini Frags) paired with Backup Mag to use during the Envious Assassin add clear phase to boost the mag up to almost all of your reserves shifted over to the one overflowed mag before swapping over to Spike Grenades, or even just something that boosts velocity. Deconstruct is also performing well when paired with the Sticky Grenades mag perk since it only takes 2 direct hits to trigger the ammo refund from Deconstruct. This means you gain essentially 50% extra total damage across your reserves, assuming you’re in a situation where you can’t easily get more heavy ammo through other means and you’re in a long encounter with a lot of necessitated heavy weapon usage. It’s a pretty niche use case that most players will not usually get much value from, since in most cases you’re using the GL for its DPS value, not for total damage, so you’d be much happier with Bait & Switch or even Explosive Light in most cases. Lastly, do not pair Deconstruct with Envious Assassin, it is an anti-combo as the ammo refund can’t trigger when the mag is above its starting point. On top of all of this you can get pretty good PvP rolls as well, where you want as much Blast Radius as you can possibly get. Easily the #1 chase priority." Masterwork: Blast Radius tags:god-pvp

// Edge Transit (pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls "Still probably on par with if not better than Cataphract due to enhanced perks. You want a mag-boosting perk (either Augmented Drum or Mini Frags) paired with Backup Mag to use during the Envious Assassin add clear phase to boost the mag up to almost all of your reserves shifted over to the one overflowed mag before swapping over to Spike Grenades, or even just something that boosts velocity. Deconstruct is also performing well when paired with the Sticky Grenades mag perk since it only takes 2 direct hits to trigger the ammo refund from Deconstruct. This means you gain essentially 50% extra total damage across your reserves, assuming you’re in a situation where you can’t easily get more heavy ammo through other means and you’re in a long encounter with a lot of necessitated heavy weapon usage. It’s a pretty niche use case that most players will not usually get much value from, since in most cases you’re using the GL for its DPS value, not for total damage, so you’d be much happier with Bait & Switch or even Explosive Light in most cases. Lastly, do not pair Deconstruct with Envious Assassin, it is an anti-combo as the ammo refund can’t trigger when the mag is above its starting point. On top of all of this you can get pretty good PvP rolls as well, where you want as much Blast Radius as you can possibly get. Easily the #1 chase priority." Masterwork: Handling, Velocity, Reload tags:pve

// Edge Transit (pvp) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvP Recommend Rolls "Still probably on par with if not better than Cataphract due to enhanced perks. You want a mag-boosting perk (either Augmented Drum or Mini Frags) paired with Backup Mag to use during the Envious Assassin add clear phase to boost the mag up to almost all of your reserves shifted over to the one overflowed mag before swapping over to Spike Grenades, or even just something that boosts velocity. Deconstruct is also performing well when paired with the Sticky Grenades mag perk since it only takes 2 direct hits to trigger the ammo refund from Deconstruct. This means you gain essentially 50% extra total damage across your reserves, assuming you’re in a situation where you can’t easily get more heavy ammo through other means and you’re in a long encounter with a lot of necessitated heavy weapon usage. It’s a pretty niche use case that most players will not usually get much value from, since in most cases you’re using the GL for its DPS value, not for total damage, so you’d be much happier with Bait & Switch or even Explosive Light in most cases. Lastly, do not pair Deconstruct with Envious Assassin, it is an anti-combo as the ammo refund can’t trigger when the mag is above its starting point. On top of all of this you can get pretty good PvP rolls as well, where you want as much Blast Radius as you can possibly get. Easily the #1 chase priority." Masterwork: Blast Radius tags:pvp

// The Recluse (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "The hype for this returning former juggernaut has died down a lot, but it should still be the best void submachine gun if you can get your hands on the right roll. Enlightened Action + Desperate Measures or Surrounded (especially good in Onslaught) for a general use weapon, or Repulsor Brace + Frenzy for Gyrfalcon Hunter. Desperate Measures seems to fall off really easily if you have volatile rounds on your weapon, so I would not recommend using that on Gyrfalcon. Due to its BiS categorization this picks up a #5 priority." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve

// Hung Jury SR4 (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommend Rolls first choice "Oh look. It’s back again. For some reason. Yay? And oof, they put the PvE  god roll of Shoot to Loot + Kinetic Tremors in the same column so you can’t get it on this one; so, right away this version of Hung Jury is strictly worse than the last Nightfall version for that reason. You can get Tremors + Firefly which is somewhat interesting, but is definitely not worth using over the previous version of the gun. For PvP they left the Box Breathing roll just as is, so this gives everyone another chance to pick up that roll - which is absolute dynamite in the crucible. For me, having the Box Breathing god roll already this drops to the bottom of the priority list (#11), but if you don’t have the Box Breathing roll you can chase it." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve

// Falling Guillotine (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "Vortex frame swords are horrible for dps right now. The heavy attack is a net dps loss as it costs 6 ammo when 4 light swings are an equivalent amount of damage. You can get double damage perks on this, but without relentless strikes your total damage will absolutely plummet since you can’t print ammo while you attack. Like so many other swords before it, this weapon with Surrounded (even when enhanced in TFS) can’t compete with Bequest simply due to Bequest’s unnatural extra 10 impact stat it has over all other swords. However, Bequest is only the top dog if you can guarantee you have Surrounded proc’d. Once you lose that then things like The Lament start coming into play - and that’s where this sword might actually come through. As long as you’re sure you can completely eschew total damage (sacrificing Relentless Strikes in column 1 for a damage perk) then the straight DPS of Frenzy/Vorpal + Bait & Switch might be a legit meta DPS option for situations where you can’t proc surrounded (e.g. Caiatl in Duality dungeon). We can speculate for the future looking at a potential buff to vortex frames or swords in general and this weapon is all upside if that winds up being the case. It may be worth picking up a roll with double damage perks just in case these ever become meta again. Calling this #9 in priority." Masterwork: Impact tags:god-pve
dimwishlist:item=243425374&perks=3666208348,269888150,4104185692,3708227201
dimwishlist:item=243425374&perks=3666208348,269888150,4104185692,3078487919

//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks "Vortex frame swords are horrible for dps right now. The heavy attack is a net dps loss as it costs 6 ammo when 4 light swings are an equivalent amount of damage. You can get double damage perks on this, but without relentless strikes your total damage will absolutely plummet since you can’t print ammo while you attack. Like so many other swords before it, this weapon with Surrounded (even when enhanced in TFS) can’t compete with Bequest simply due to Bequest’s unnatural extra 10 impact stat it has over all other swords. However, Bequest is only the top dog if you can guarantee you have Surrounded proc’d. Once you lose that then things like The Lament start coming into play - and that’s where this sword might actually come through. As long as you’re sure you can completely eschew total damage (sacrificing Relentless Strikes in column 1 for a damage perk) then the straight DPS of Frenzy/Vorpal + Bait & Switch might be a legit meta DPS option for situations where you can’t proc surrounded (e.g. Caiatl in Duality dungeon). We can speculate for the future looking at a potential buff to vortex frames or swords in general and this weapon is all upside if that winds up being the case. It may be worth picking up a roll with double damage perks just in case these ever become meta again. Calling this #9 in priority." Masterwork: Impact tags:pve

// Hammerhead (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "I was really excited for this gun to come back and it came back strong in some ways and mediocre in others. As the standard “void MG” it cannot compete with Commemoration. Reconstruction + Killing Tally on that gun can’t be beaten by anything this gun can do. Rewind Rounds is a pale shadow of Reconstruction, Bray Inheritance is way stronger than Indomitability. However, this can roll double lethality perks in the forms of Rampage in column 1 plus Onslaught or Killing Tally in column 2. Specifically on Void Hunter, and Hunter in general for that matter, you can use dodge to bypass the truly odious reload time of a machine gun and maintain the massive damage capability of the double damage perks. Sadly, Hunter dodge will reset Killing Tally, but that’s not necessarily the end of the world. It can also get a pretty good counter-meta PvP roll as well. // Blast Furnace (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommended Perks first choice "Aggressive Bursts have been in a weird place for awhile in Destiny. The deterministic recoil on this weapon will be the main factor in whether or not this is usable in PvP. If it is usable this should wind up being a very solid gun, along the lines of a Belisarius-D. For PvE there is basically just one roll you’d be looking for with Kinetic Tremors and Frenzy, and that may very well be good enough to break into high-end content over the likes of a perfect Battle Scar. The combination of the QoL buffs and damage from Frenzy, the enhanced perks (once TFS launches), and the origin trait being better may all place this above a classic Shoot to Loot + Tremors pulse like Battle Scar. If you like the gun it should be a fun nostalgic weapon to pick up and use. #6 priority, middle of the pack." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve

// Blast Furnace (pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Recommended Perks "Aggressive Bursts have been in a weird place for awhile in Destiny. The deterministic recoil on this weapon will be the main factor in whether or not this is usable in PvP. If it is usable this should wind up being a very solid gun, along the lines of a Belisarius-D. For PvE there is basically just one roll you’d be looking for with Kinetic Tremors and Frenzy, and that may very well be good enough to break into high-end content over the likes of a perfect Battle Scar. The combination of the QoL buffs and damage from Frenzy, the enhanced perks (once TFS launches), and the origin trait being better may all place this above a classic Shoot to Loot + Tremors pulse like Battle Scar. If you like the gun it should be a fun nostalgic weapon to pick up and use. #6 priority, middle of the pack." Masterwork: Reload tags:pve

// Blast Furnace (pvp) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvP Recommended Perks "Aggressive Bursts have been in a weird place for awhile in Destiny. The deterministic recoil on this weapon will be the main factor in whether or not this is usable in PvP. If it is usable this should wind up being a very solid gun, along the lines of a Belisarius-D. For PvE there is basically just one roll you’d be looking for with Kinetic Tremors and Frenzy, and that may very well be good enough to break into high-end content over the likes of a perfect Battle Scar. The combination of the QoL buffs and damage from Frenzy, the enhanced perks (once TFS launches), and the origin trait being better may all place this above a classic Shoot to Loot + Tremors pulse like Battle Scar. If you like the gun it should be a fun nostalgic weapon to pick up and use. #6 priority, middle of the pack." Masterwork: Range, Handling, Stability tags:pvp

// Elsie's Rifle (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "Tough weapon to judge for PvE. On the surface it looks underwhelming, but there are some interesting perks in here to note. I should also note that this weapon has literally double the base reload of the rest of its archetype. 60 base reload is insane here and should not be overlooked. Perks-wise this has some ok perks for clearing low-level content like Desperate Measures, Kill Clip, and Adrenaline Junkie, but the fact that this is a void weapon hurts the use case for all of those due to subclass limitations. That leaves Frenzy as the premiere choice for high-end content and oh boy Under-Over and Repulsor Brace as pairings are super juicy here. Under-Over would be ideal for the next time we get an anti-barrier season and Repulsor Brace should be the far more ubiquitous choice for Gyrfalcon Hunter. Overall though this archetype isn’t really used much in PvE. For PvP this is an absolute monster of a weapon. Elsie’s can hit max range with the aid of Keep Away and looks like it could be very, very strong - unfortunately the deterministic recoil pattern is horrible on this weapon. Do not run a counterbalance mod, in any configuration it just pulls the recoil poorly. You need one of the 3 recoil-adjusting barrel perks to make this usable at all, preferably Extended Barrel being the premiere choice. The base stats on Elsie’s are huge. It’s like having a Messenger with 3 adept mods already on it (2 in reload, 1 in handling). Overall, this is looking like a great chase for PvP, so making it a #4 prio." Masterwork: Reload tags:god-pve
dimwishlist:item=3851176026&perks=839105230,3230963543,1870851715,4104185692
dimwishlist:item=3851176026&perks=1467527085,3230963543,1870851715,4104185692


// Elsie's Rifle (god-pvp) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvP Perks first choice "Tough weapon to judge for PvE. On the surface it looks underwhelming, but there are some interesting perks in here to note. I should also note that this weapon has literally double the base reload of the rest of its archetype. 60 base reload is insane here and should not be overlooked. Perks-wise this has some ok perks for clearing low-level content like Desperate Measures, Kill Clip, and Adrenaline Junkie, but the fact that this is a void weapon hurts the use case for all of those due to subclass limitations. That leaves Frenzy as the premiere choice for high-end content and oh boy Under-Over and Repulsor Brace as pairings are super juicy here. Under-Over would be ideal for the next time we get an anti-barrier season and Repulsor Brace should be the far more ubiquitous choice for Gyrfalcon Hunter. Overall though this archetype isn’t really used much in PvE. For PvP this is an absolute monster of a weapon. Elsie’s can hit max range with the aid of Keep Away and looks like it could be very, very strong - unfortunately the deterministic recoil pattern is horrible on this weapon. Do not run a counterbalance mod, in any configuration it just pulls the recoil poorly. You need one of the 3 recoil-adjusting barrel perks to make this usable at all, preferably Extended Barrel being the premiere choice. The base stats on Elsie’s are huge. It’s like having a Messenger with 3 adept mods already on it (2 in reload, 1 in handling). Overall, this is looking like a great chase for PvP, so making it a #4 prio." Masterwork: Range tags:god-pvp

// Elsie's Rifle (pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks "Tough weapon to judge for PvE. On the surface it looks underwhelming, but there are some interesting perks in here to note. I should also note that this weapon has literally double the base reload of the rest of its archetype. 60 base reload is insane here and should not be overlooked. Perks-wise this has some ok perks for clearing low-level content like Desperate Measures, Kill Clip, and Adrenaline Junkie, but the fact that this is a void weapon hurts the use case for all of those due to subclass limitations. That leaves Frenzy as the premiere choice for high-end content and oh boy Under-Over and Repulsor Brace as pairings are super juicy here. Under-Over would be ideal for the next time we get an anti-barrier season and Repulsor Brace should be the far more ubiquitous choice for Gyrfalcon Hunter. Overall though this archetype isn’t really used much in PvE. For PvP this is an absolute monster of a weapon. Elsie’s can hit max range with the aid of Keep Away and looks like it could be very, very strong - unfortunately the deterministic recoil pattern is horrible on this weapon. Do not run a counterbalance mod, in any configuration it just pulls the recoil poorly. You need one of the 3 recoil-adjusting barrel perks to make this usable at all, preferably Extended Barrel being the premiere choice. The base stats on Elsie’s are huge. It’s like having a Messenger with 3 adept mods already on it (2 in reload, 1 in handling). Overall, this is looking like a great chase for PvP, so making it a #4 prio." Masterwork: Reload, Handling tags:pve

// Elsie's Rifle (pvp) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvP Perks "Tough weapon to judge for PvE. On the surface it looks underwhelming, but there are some interesting perks in here to note. I should also note that this weapon has literally double the base reload of the rest of its archetype. 60 base reload is insane here and should not be overlooked. Perks-wise this has some ok perks for clearing low-level content like Desperate Measures, Kill Clip, and Adrenaline Junkie, but the fact that this is a void weapon hurts the use case for all of those due to subclass limitations. That leaves Frenzy as the premiere choice for high-end content and oh boy Under-Over and Repulsor Brace as pairings are super juicy here. Under-Over would be ideal for the next time we get an anti-barrier season and Repulsor Brace should be the far more ubiquitous choice for Gyrfalcon Hunter. Overall though this archetype isn’t really used much in PvE. For PvP this is an absolute monster of a weapon. Elsie’s can hit max range with the aid of Keep Away and looks like it could be very, very strong - unfortunately the deterministic recoil pattern is horrible on this weapon. Do not run a counterbalance mod, in any configuration it just pulls the recoil poorly. You need one of the 3 recoil-adjusting barrel perks to make this usable at all, preferably Extended Barrel being the premiere choice. The base stats on Elsie’s are huge. It’s like having a Messenger with 3 adept mods already on it (2 in reload, 1 in handling). Overall, this is looking like a great chase for PvP, so making it a #4 prio." Masterwork: Range tags:pvp

// Midnight Coup () (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "The return of one of the best weapons from Y1 of D2. They’ve buffed the base stat package here and juiced up the perk pool. This should supplant Fatebringer (even the timelost versions) as the premiere PvE kinetic slot handcannon for high-end content. Deterministic recoil here really sucks, and neither of the +10 barrels actually fixes it, so you’d just be looking for Arrowhead Brake. The biggest chase should be Shoot to Loot + Kinetic Tremors, but Attrition Orbs (the tremors count to attrition stacks) paired with Tremors is also a dynamite roll I’d suggest keeping as well. The weapon needs reload help at base to help it out. I’d recommend at least 71 (maybe 66) in reload stat, but you’d really be happy with 81. This makes the jump in reload from a Firefly proc fairly meaningless, and the actual damage from a firefly proc is pretty lackluster in a small radius (especially in high-end content), so even though people are going nuts over it I honestly wouldn’t recommend it. The best current roll then would be to go for either Explosive Payload + Frenzy or one of the Kinetic Tremors rolls mentioned above (EP, Attrition, or Shoot). For the classic Fatebringer roll (EP+Frenzy) this weapon has worse stats (Range & Stab since Frenzy maxes out Handling and Reload), but the perks can be enhanced and it has a pretty good origin trait compared to the rather meaningless adept mods that Fatebringer can get on its Timelost version. Without Arrowhead Brake though this weapon won’t feel as good as Fatebringer does. Tough to get a good roll on this since you need the perk combo AND reload help AND arrowhead brake. This is high priority (#3)." Masterwork: Reload

// Midnight Coup () (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks "The return of one of the best weapons from Y1 of D2. They’ve buffed the base stat package here and juiced up the perk pool. This should supplant Fatebringer (even the timelost versions) as the premiere PvE kinetic slot handcannon for high-end content. Deterministic recoil here really sucks, and neither of the +10 barrels actually fixes it, so you’d just be looking for Arrowhead Brake. The biggest chase should be Shoot to Loot + Kinetic Tremors, but Attrition Orbs (the tremors count to attrition stacks) paired with Tremors is also a dynamite roll I’d suggest keeping as well. The weapon needs reload help at base to help it out. I’d recommend at least 71 (maybe 66) in reload stat, but you’d really be happy with 81. This makes the jump in reload from a Firefly proc fairly meaningless, and the actual damage from a firefly proc is pretty lackluster in a small radius (especially in high-end content), so even though people are going nuts over it I honestly wouldn’t recommend it. The best current roll then would be to go for either Explosive Payload + Frenzy or one of the Kinetic Tremors rolls mentioned above (EP, Attrition, or Shoot). For the classic Fatebringer roll (EP+Frenzy) this weapon has worse stats (Range & Stab since Frenzy maxes out Handling and Reload), but the perks can be enhanced and it has a pretty good origin trait compared to the rather meaningless adept mods that Fatebringer can get on its Timelost version. Without Arrowhead Brake though this weapon won’t feel as good as Fatebringer does. Tough to get a good roll on this since you need the perk combo AND reload help AND arrowhead brake. This is high priority (#3)." Masterwork: Reload

// Succession (god-pve) (Holofoil)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks first choice "Oof. From the top to the bottom of these new weapons. There is actually no reason to get this gun at all. The raid version is strictly better in every way as this brings no better or more interesting perk pairings, and the Bray Inheritance origin trait is just a better version of Indomitability. The only thing that could be said here is that Discord is at least something different in perk slot 1, but you’d have to eschew Reconstruction for that, and ultimately what would be the point? I get that it prints free ammo, but why are you using an aggressive sniper rifle for add clear? This weapon makes no sense to reissue and should be the only hard avoid on the list. #12 and it isn’t close. " Masterwork: Handling tags:god-pve

title:S23 Prophecy Random Roll Weapons
description:The Origin trait here is called Crossing Over, and it is mostly forgettable. Its effect is negligible PvE and is a decent passive benefit in PvP, but nothing that pushes these weapons over the top on its own.

// Darkest Before (pve)
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) PvE Perks "Best in class stats across the board, but there are many reasons why this weapon is way behind most other primaries you could choose. Unfortunately this pulse has deterministic recoil which is extremely unfortunate on one of the most punishing archetypes in the entire game for recoil direction. Also, the way the sandbox has shifted this weapon has the same optimal ttk as many auto rifles and actually gets outranged by most of them. For PvP this is likely a nonstarter, especially since you have to basically get a perfect roll in order to be competitive at base. For PvE this can get some fine rolls, but is unfortunately outclassed entirely by Adhortative and other solar pulses. Not being craftable also makes this pretty much pointless to farm." Masterwork: Reload tags:pve

// Tusk of the Boar ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "This is the actual best weapon we’re getting this midseason update. The stats on this are so high, including the Field-Tested origin trait (which will stack up quickly due to the nature of the weapon) that you don’t necessarily need Enlightened Action or to make up for missing stats in many places on the weapon. The base reload of the gun plus the origin trait means that you really won’t notice much of the effects of Enlightened Action if you happen to roll that saly. Slice is a nifty trick in perk 1 slot, and slideways is also good. But the real juice is Envious Assassin. At first it may seem like the perk is at odds with the nature of an add clear weapon, but all it takes is 1 kill to refill a round, so right off the bat at worst this perk is autoloading holster, and at best it can fill up to 3 shots in the mag. Deconstruct is where things really get interesting. This means the gun can reload itself out of thin air directly into the mag. It won’t have the AOE capability of Chain Reaction, but that is being nerfed with TFS. Hatchling is an option for warlock builds." Masterwork: Reload, Handling

// Tusk of the Boar ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks "This is the actual best weapon we’re getting this midseason update. The stats on this are so high, including the Field-Tested origin trait (which will stack up quickly due to the nature of the weapon) that you don’t necessarily need Enlightened Action or to make up for missing stats in many places on the weapon. The base reload of the gun plus the origin trait means that you really won’t notice much of the effects of Enlightened Action if you happen to roll that saly. Slice is a nifty trick in perk 1 slot, and slideways is also good. But the real juice is Envious Assassin. At first it may seem like the perk is at odds with the nature of an add clear weapon, but all it takes is 1 kill to refill a round, so right off the bat at worst this perk is autoloading holster, and at best it can fill up to 3 shots in the mag. Deconstruct is where things really get interesting. This means the gun can reload itself out of thin air directly into the mag. It won’t have the AOE capability of Chain Reaction, but that is being nerfed with TFS. Hatchling is an option for warlock builds." Masterwork: Reload, Handling, Velocity

// The Slammer (Adept) ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "One of the most interesting weapons released in a long time. Bait and Switch is absolute bait right now. Going for a DPS roll on this archetype is a trap as Vortex frames are hilariously terrible for damage currently (the heavy attack costs 6(!) ammo so you’re way better off spamming light attacks) and are so far behind normal adaptives, let alone Bequest, that is just isn’t worth pretending it is good right now. If you have the patience and the vault space it is probably worth keeping a Bait & Switch roll for any future buffs they give to vortex frames though. For general use, Cold Steel is really cool since it can CC mobs, but also stun both overload and unstoppable champions if you are brave enough (the Stunning Recovery origin trait will heal you once you proc the stun, but you have to survive long enough to get it!). Unlike most other swords you want to prioritize ammo over damage for an Eager Edge/Chain Reaction + Cold Steel/Demo roll." Masterwork: Impact 
dimwishlist:item=1354727549&perks=1261178282,269888150,2077819806,3650930298

// The Slammer ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "One of the most interesting weapons released in a long time. Bait and Switch is absolute bait right now. Going for a DPS roll on this archetype is a trap as Vortex frames are hilariously terrible for damage currently (the heavy attack costs 6(!) ammo so you’re way better off spamming light attacks) and are so far behind normal adaptives, let alone Bequest, that is just isn’t worth pretending it is good right now. If you have the patience and the vault space it is probably worth keeping a Bait & Switch roll for any future buffs they give to vortex frames though. For general use, Cold Steel is really cool since it can CC mobs, but also stun both overload and unstoppable champions if you are brave enough (the Stunning Recovery origin trait will heal you once you proc the stun, but you have to survive long enough to get it!). Unlike most other swords you want to prioritize ammo over damage for an Eager Edge/Chain Reaction + Cold Steel/Demo roll." Masterwork: Impact 
dimwishlist:item=2889501828&perks=1261178282,269888150,2077819806,3650930298

// Multimach CCX ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "This is one of the best weapons we’re getting in the mid-season update. The Field-Tested Origin Trait is fantastic on a fast-firing SMG like this, as well as the proc from Kinetic Tremors coming into play there. The biggest drawbacks are going to be Reload (without a proper Perk 1 since we’re going Attrition Orbs) and Range. You need to strike a balance between the two stats in order for this to really shine, and remember that it will be super easy to hit 1 or 2 stacks of Field-Tested almost immediately which provides meaningful bonuses to both of the stats we’re targeting. Attrition Orbs here makes this a unique weapon off the bat as an absurd orb battery, but you can go for Under-Over if you want a good option for the next time SMGs have Barrier-breaking capability from the artifact." Masterwork: Reload

//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks first choice "This is incredibly exciting and new. The journey for Heavy Wave GLs has been quite something as when the first one launched with Lightfall it was just a creative way to blow yourself up. NOW they are becoming incredible for add clear, rivaling if not surpassing Machine Guns, and there is an upcoming 30% buff to chain reaction on Heavy Wave GLs in TFS that should make this absolutely unrivaled for massive add clear. Voltshot can roll in the perk 1 slot, but is not really very interesting as you can only improve reload on the masterwork which is a 1 out of 5 chance and only gets the gun to barely 50 reload. Even then the purpose of Voltshot is add clear, which the weapon is already incredible at, so there really isn’t any point in going for that. Blast Radius only affects the initial explosion before the wave goes out, so the value of that stat is overhyped on this weapon. Handling is really the true giga-stat for Hullabaloo when paired with Autoloader or Envious Assassin." Masterwork: Handling

// Supercluster ()

title:Dawning 2023 Weapons
description:The Origin trait for these weapons just grants you a dawning gift. This leaves a small purple cube on the ground that heals you and restores energy when picked up. It’s basically a Wellspring proc combined with a Recuperation proc. In general, that is pretty nice, and you don’t really need to think about it. Most of these weapons have multiple origin traits so you can switch over to Hakke, Suros, or Omolon as well.

// Stay Frosty - Recommended Perks ()
//notes: SpaceMonkey's Weapon Guide (https://docs.google.com/document/d/1KGxePntz2loCYlAhdKm0fJyyf_YURJ1Zd7L1smsu4-c) Recommended Perks "This is one of my favorite archetypes, but the muzzle flash on this gun makes it borderline unusable. I’m not sure Bungie will ever fix it as it has had this problem for a long time now and they have not addressed it. The stats on this are very comparable to others, so it doesn’t need a ton of help anywhere, just good stat bumps where you want it. For PvP you want Arrowhead Brake+Counterbalance mod to get to 100 recoil. A lightweight frame with Headstone and Desperado is really cool in PvE, and all you “need” beyond that is Arrowhead Brake so you can actually hit those crits reliably. But again, with that horrible muzzle flash effect taking up the entire screen I can’t in good conscience recommend this gun." Masterwork: Stability, Range
